He had a fever, diarrhea and vomiting after playing for an afternoon. After asking the front desk, they agreed very happily, which was just right for the child to have a good rest. name:X‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçp‚Äça‚Äçn
info:River-view Twin Room
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Business travelers
info:9 Reviews
rating:4.5
posted:Posted March 31, 2024
msg:In most cases, I would give full marks, but this time I want to deduct points for the service of the hotel front desk.
Let me talk about the advantages first: the location is good, right by the Yangtze River, close to the pedestrian street, and it is very convenient to eat and drink. It is also convenient to get to the hotel from Changjiu Expressway. The breakfast is good, with many options (except for the lack of cheese and butter), which is satisfactory.
Special advantages: The room service must be praised. I stayed for two nights in a row, and there was a room turndown service for both nights: slippers were taken, curtains were tidied, and fruit yogurt and honey were sent. These are not available in many first-line brands of five-star hotels. Thumbs up.
Serious criticism: The front desk should be criticized. When checking in, I asked about the parking and exit regulations, which were different from the actual operation on the second day. On the second day, I was asked to fill in the license plate number in the front desk form. On the third day, when I checked out, my car could not leave the parking lot because the license plate was not entered into the system for me. This is not a big deal, but it caused me a lot of trouble, and the business feeling left was very bad, so that now it has been three days since I checked out, and I still have to point out this shortcoming. I hope the hotel will improve.
